=== SEARCH SNIPPETS ===

[45 Eugenia - Wikipedia]
Discovery Eugenia was discovered on 27 June 1857 by the Franco–German amateur astronomer Hermann Goldschmidt. [12] His instrument of discovery was a 4-inch aperture telescope located in his sixth floor apartment in the 6th arrondissement of Paris. [13] It was the 45th minor planet to be discovered.
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/45_Eugenia

[45 Eugenia - Wikiwand]
Discovery Eugenia was discovered on 27 June 1857 by the Franco–German amateur astronomer Hermann Goldschmidt. [12] His instrument of discovery was a 4-inch aperture telescope located in his sixth floor apartment in the 6th arrondissement of Paris. [13] It was the 45th minor planet to be discovered.
URL: https://www.wikiwand.com/en/articles/45_Eugenia

[Images of a Capital The Impressionists in Paris]
Between 1894 and 1898, he erected the Castel Béranger, a large building in the 16th arrondissement, in which apartments were available for a reasonable rent. ...
URL: https://pmalibrary.org/digitized/wp-content/uploads/2018/11/MF_ImagesofaCapital_Essays_2010_000008184.pdf

[45 Eugenia Explained]
Nov 26, 2005 · Discovery Eugenia was discovered on 27 June 1857 by the Franco-German amateur astronomer Hermann Goldschmidt. His instrument of discovery was a 4-inch aperture telescope located in his sixth floor apartment in the 6th Arrondissement of Paris. It was the forty-fifth minor planet to be discovered.
URL: https://everything.explained.today/%5C/45_Eugenia/


=== FULL EXTRACTED CONTENT ===


--- [45 Eugenia - Wikipedia] ---
45 Eugenia is a large asteroid of the asteroid belt. It is famed as one of the first asteroids to be found to have a moon orbiting it. It was also the second triple asteroid to be discovered, after 87 Sylvia.
